c\u1ee7a Bitcoin hi\u1ec7n \u1edf m\u1ee9c 49,58%, g\u1ea7n g\u1ea5p ba l\u1ea7n s\u1ef1 th\u1ed1ng tr\u1ecb c\u1ee7a Ethereum (ETH), lo\u1ea1i ti\u1ec1n \u0111i\u1ec7n t\u1eed l\u1edbn th\u1ee9 hai t\u00ednh theo v\u1ed1n h\u00f3a th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng, \u1edf m\u1ee9c kho\u1ea3ng 16,7%.\n\nS\u1ef1 gia t\u0103ng th\u1ed1ng tr\u1ecb \u1ed5n \u0111\u1ecbnh n\u00e0y, b\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u c\u1ee7a Bitcoin ph\u1ea7n l\u1edbn c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 l\u00e0 do s\u1ef1 ph\u1ee5c h\u1ed3i k\u00e9o d\u00e0i m\u1ed9t n\u0103m c\u1ee7a n\u00f3, v\u1edbi gi\u00e1 ti\u1ec1n \u0111i\u1ec7n t\u1eed \u0111\u00e3 t\u0103ng 81% k\u1ec3 t\u1eeb \u0111\u1ea7u n\u0103m 2023.\n\nHi\u1ec7u su\u1ea5t \u1ea5n t\u01b0\u1ee3ng n\u00e0y \u0111\u00e3 c\u1ee7ng c\u1ed1 v\u1ecb th\u1ebf c\u1ee7a Bitcoin Many investors utilize risk/reward ratios to assess the expected returns of an investment relative to the level of risk they must assume to achieve those returns. A lower risk/return ratio is typically more favorable, as it indicates less risk for an equivalent potential gain.  Let's consider an example: an investment with a risk-reward ratio of 1:7 implies that an investor is willing to risk $1 for the opportunity to earn $7. In contrast, a risk/reward ratio of 1:3 suggests that an investor should expect to invest $1 in order to potentially earn $3 on their investment.
